============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO21)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(x,t,v)=0.767518260471059\,\sin(t)\;-\;0.263896435020576\,v\sin(x).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (possibly after setting some candidate constants to 0) to produce **(i)** a pure \(\sin(t)\) term with constant amplitude, and **(ii)** a term proportional to \(v\sin(x)\) with constant coefficient, and **(iii)** no other dependence on \(x,t,v\) on the chosen domain.

I check each candidate for whether it even has the right “building blocks” (a standalone \(\sin(t)\) and a \(v\sin(x)\) interaction). If a required structure is absent, no choice of constants can create it.

---

### 1.
Has \( \exp(c3\cos(c4 t))\) and \( \exp(c7|v|)\sin(c8 t+c9)\), plus linear-in-\(x\) terms. No \(\sin(x)\) anywhere, and the only sine is in \(t\) multiplied by \(\exp(c7|v|)\) (depends on \(v\) unless \(c7=0\), but then it’s just \(\sin(t+\phi)\) with no \(v\sin(x)\) term). Cannot form \(-\beta v\sin(x)\). **No.**

### 2.
Similar: sines only in \(t\) inside an exponential; no \(\sin(x)\), no \(v\sin(x)\). **No.**

### 3.
Has \(x\sin(c7 t+c8)\) (sine in \(t\) multiplied by \(x\)), and exponentials; no \(\sin(x)\), no \(v\sin(x)\). **No.**

### 4.
Has \(x\cos(c6 t)\) and \(\cos(c8 t+c9)\); no \(\sin(t)\) unless via phase shift from cosine (possible), but still no \(\sin(x)\) and no \(v\sin(x)\). **No.**

### 5.

GT Equivalence Verification (PO21)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v = 0.7675*sin(t) - 0.2639*v*sin(x)**

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to sin(t)
2. A term proportional to v*sin(x)

Let me analyze each candidate to see if it can match this form.

### Key observations about GT:
- It contains sin(t) — a sinusoidal function of t
- It contains v*sin(x) — product of v with sin(x)
- No polynomial terms in x, no exponential terms, no v² or v³ terms

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*exp(c3*cos(c4*t)) + c5*x + c6*exp(c7*Abs(v))*sin(c8*t + c9)`
Contains exp(c7*Abs(v)) which can't be eliminated (it multiplies sin). No v*sin(x) term. Setting c7=0 gives c6*sin(c8*t+c9) for the t-dependent part, but still no v*sin(x) term. The x terms are linear, not sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*exp(c3*cos(c4*t)) + c5*x + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*t + c9))`
No v dependence at all. GT depends on v. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*exp(c4*x + c5*t) + c6*x*sin(c7*t + c8)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x**c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*x*cos(c6*t) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 5:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x*cos(c3*t) + c4*v/(c5 + Abs(v)) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`
Has v/(c5+Abs(v)) which is not v*sin(x). The v dependence is wrong — it's a function of v only, not v*sin(x). Can't produce v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 6:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*x + c4*v*cos(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7*cos(c8*t + c9))`
Has v*cos(c5*t) — this is v times a function of t, not v*sin(x). Can't produce v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 7:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x**c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*x + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 8:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*exp(c6*t) + c7*x*cos(c8*t)`
Has v**3 not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 9:** `c0*x**c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6)) + c7*sin(c8*t + c9)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 10:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2 + c3*x**c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*t + c8))`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 11:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*v**3 + c3*v + c4 + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*cos(c7*t + c8)`
Has c3*v (linear in v, no x dependence — not v*sin(x)). Has cos(c7*t+c8) for t part. To match GT: need v*sin(x) but only has v (no sin(x) factor). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 12:** `c0*x**c1 + c2 + c3*x**c4 + c5*v/sqrt(c6 + v**2) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
v/sqrt(c6+v²) is not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 13:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*v**3 + c3*v + c4 + c5*x**c6*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9*v*Abs(v)`
Has c3*v (not v*sin(x)), and x**c6*sin(c7*t+c8) (not sin(t) alone or v*sin(x)). Can't match. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 14:** `c0/x**5 + c1 + c2/x**4 + c3*x**c4 + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
Has v*Abs(v) not v*sin(x). Since v takes both signs, v*Abs(v) ≠ c*v. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 15:** `c0/x**5 + c1 + c2*x**c3 + c4*v**c5 + c6*exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t + c9)`
v**c5: if c5=1, this is c4*v (not v*sin(x)). exp(c7*x)*sin(c8*t+c9) mixes x and t but not as sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 16:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*v*Abs(v) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t + c7)`
v*Abs(v) ≠ v*sin(x). exp(c5*t)*sin(c6*t+c7) ≠ sin(t) unless c5=0. If c5=0: sin(c6*t+c7). But v*Abs(v) can't become v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 17:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2*(Abs(c3*v) + 1)**3 + c4*cos(c5*t + c6)`
(Abs(c3*v)+1)³ expands to terms with Abs(v)³, Abs(v)², Abs(v), and constants. Not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 18:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*cos(c3*log(c4*Abs(x) + 1)) + c5*v*exp(c6*x) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
Has c5*v*exp(c6*x) — this is v times exp(c6*x), not v*sin(x). exp(c6*x) ≠ sin(x) for any constant. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 19:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*v**3 + c3*v + c4 + c5*x**c6*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9*v`
Same as 13 essentially (c3*v + c9*v = (c3+c9)*v). Still v not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 20:** `c0/x**5 + c1*v**3 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6)) + c7*v`
c7*v is linear in v but not v*sin(x). exp(c4*sin(...)) ≠ sin(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 21:** `c0/x**5 + c1 + c2*x**(1/3) + c3*v**3 + c4*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*x`
Has v**3 not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 22:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*cos(c3*t + c4)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 23:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*x + c5`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 24:** `c0*x/(c1 + c2*exp(c3*x)) + c4*x**c5*sin(c6*t + c7)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 25:** `c0*x**c1 + c2*v**3 + c3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t + c7)) + c8*v`
c8*v not v*sin(x). exp(c5*sin(...)) ≠ sin(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 26:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)*cos(c4*x) + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*t) + c8*v + 1)`
The log term mixes v and t nonlinearly. Can't separate into v*sin(x) + sin(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 27:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*x + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t + c7))`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 28:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*exp(c6*t) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)`
v**3 not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 29:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x + c6*t) + c7*v*x**c8`
Has c7*v*x**c8. Could this be v*sin(x)? No — x**c8 is a power function, not sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 30:** `c0*x/(c1 + c2*exp(c3*x)) + c4*log(c5*x + c6*exp(c7*t) + 1)`
No v dependence. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 31:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*exp(c6*t) + c7*v*Max(0, -v) + c7*v*Max(0, v)`
Note: v*Max(0,-v) + v*Max(0,v). When v>0: v*0 + v*v = v². When v<0: v*(-v) + v*0 = -v² = -v². So this is v*|v| = v*Abs(v), not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 32:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**2 + c4*v**3 + c5*exp(c6*x)*exp(c7*t) + c8`
No v*sin(x) term. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 33:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*exp(c6*t) + c7*x`
No sin(t), no v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 34:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*exp(c6*t) + c7*v`
c7*v not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 35:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + x)) + c3*v + c4*v**3 + c5*exp(c6*x + c7*t)`
c3*v not v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 36-50:** Let me check remaining ones quickly for v*sin(x) and sin(t) terms.

**Candidates 36-50:** None contain sin(x) as a basis function, and none have v*sin(x). They all have v in polynomial forms (v, v², v³, v*Abs(v)) or other non-sin(x) combinations.

After checking all 50 candidates: **None** contain the term v*sin(x), which is essential for matching the GT. The GT requires sin(x) as a basis function, and no candidate includes it.
